2026-01-17 12:49:01.054 | â”‚ S2|H|S1|Behavior niche grid hypothesis. X-axis (execution modality): (1) Static=notebook runs once, produces output (2) Reactive=notebook responds to events/triggers (3) Agentic=notebook has goals, makes decisions, loops (4) Swarm=multiple notebook instances coordinate. Y-axis (integration): (1) Isolated=pure compute, no external deps (2) Observatory=streams state via WS to visualization (3) Container=spawns sandboxed processes (4) Multi-system=orchestrates external services. This gives 16 primary niches. Each can have sub-niches by domain. Starting w/ high-value unexplored regions.   â”‚

Fitness function notebook evaluates (tests pass, perf metrics, code quality). Selection+mutation: top performers spawn variants, bottom pruned. Observable via Observatory: fitness landscape visualization, lineage trees, convergence metrics. Meta-level: notebooks evolving notebooks. Could use container-use for sandboxed execution of generated code.   â”‚

Unlike static notebooks (run once) or pure reactive (respond in-process), these spawn isolated execution environments. Key enabler: container-use MCP server. Observable via: Observatory app channel (preview:status, preview:log). High novelty bc combines event-driven + sandboxed execution.   â”‚

Notebook orchestrates: (1) Firecrawl scrapes sources (2) Container runs data transformation (3) Database write via MCP (4) Slack notification on completion. Thoughtbox handles: schema inference, data quality checks, error recovery decisions, anomaly detection. Observable: pipeline DAG, data samples at each stage, AI reasoning about quality. Diff from Airflow: embedded reasoning, visual debugging, adaptive error handling.   â”‚

Continuous notebook: (1) Fetches API specs from multiple providers (OpenAPI/GraphQL) (2) Compares against local client code (3) Detects breaking changes, deprecations (4) Generates migration guides. Thoughtbox: reasons about semantic breaking vs. syntactic, prioritizes by usage patterns, drafts PRs. Observable: API diff visualization, impact analysis, migration roadmap. Use case: microservice ecosystems, third-party integrations.   â”‚

Identifies: (1) Redundant reasoning loops (2) Missed branching opportunities (3) Premature convergence (4) Under-explored hypotheses. Generates: optimized reasoning templates, better prompts, pattern recommendations. Observable: reasoning topology analysis, optimization suggestions, before/after comparison. Self-improvement loop: optimizer improves own reasoning patterns. Connects to DGM/CycleQD evolution in memory system.   â”‚

When notebook execution fails: (1) Parses error + stack trace (2) Reads notebook source as data (3) Uses Thoughtbox to hypothesize root cause (4) Generates fix candidates (5) Tests fixes in container. 2026-01-17 12:52:01.852 | â”‚ S25|H|S20|Meta-notebook Phenotype D5: 'Notebook Evolver' (connects to A3 evolutionary swarm). Population of notebook variants. Fitness: execution success, output quality, resource efficiency, code clarity. Selection: top performers breed. Mutation: cell reordering, dep changes, logic tweaks. Crossover: merge cells from different parents. Observable: fitness landscape, lineage tree, Pareto frontier. Key: notebooks as genotypes, behaviors as phenotypes. Notebook reads codebase, streams comprehension to Observatory at human-readable pace. User watches AI 'understand' their code. 2026-01-17 12:52:47.536 | â”‚ S31|H|S27|Observatory Phenotype E4: 'Ambient Awareness Display'. Always-on notebook streams context to ambient display (second monitor, wall screen, mobile widget). Shows: project health, recent commits, open issues, team activity. Thoughtbox: prioritizes what's attention-worthy, filters noise, highlights anomalies. Observable: glanceable cards, priority indicators, contextual alerts. Use case: team rooms, personal dashboards, manager views. Background awareness w/o active monitoring.   â”‚

Multiple notebooks: (1) Crawl codebase, generate docs (2) Analyze doc quality, identify gaps (3) Research best practices, compare (4) Improve doc generation (5) Track reader behavior, optimize for comprehension. On incident: (1) Reads runbook steps (2) Executes each in container (3) Observes results (4) Makes decisions on conditional branches (5) Escalates when uncertain. B's cells become callable functions in A. Observable: composition graph, execution flow across notebooks. Enables: (1) Reusable reasoning patterns (2) Library of notebook primitives (3) Higher-order notebooks that orchestrate others. Like npm for notebooks. Technical: extend .src.md with import syntax, resolve at runtime.   â”‚

Enables: (1) Resumable reasoning (2) Branching from historical states (3) Reasoning playback/replay. Technical: serialize Thoughtbox session to JSON, store in notebook metadata or external store.
